	<h1 class="hl ">
						ALL THAT POWER AND IMPRESSIVE MPG?</h1>	
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						</div>
				</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="parbase cnt_imgpar_c1 section"><div class="mds-cmp-content01 cnt_mmpar_1  mod modCnt_mmpar_1 ">
	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>It starts when you get that first glance of the unmistakable design. Those deep-set eyes, the rear shoulders sculpted from an impressive one-piece, body side panel. Oh, there’s an immediate chemistry alright. But it’s on that first real driving date that you’ll really be hooked — because Camaro Coupe’s beauty isn’t only skin deep.<br>
<br>
It’s the 323-horsepower V6. Or the massive boost behind the 426-horsepower V8 available on SS, including the SS with the track-ready 1LE Performance Package. It’s the excitement of the precision handling that comes with 4-wheel independent suspension and world class braking you can’t get on a Mustang. The smart and accessible technology you’ll find inside. It won’t take you long to realize that this one is different from all the other cars you’ve driven before.<br>
<br>
By the time you uncover the accessible price, the EPA-estimated 30 MPG highway for 2LS, the available 7-inch diagonal touch-screen and the available Head-Up Display projected on your windshield, there’ll be no turning back. This really was meant to be.<br>
&nbsp;<br>
The 2013 Camaro has been recognized by J.D. Power as the “Highest Ranked Midsize Sporty Car in Initial Quality in a <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_15" class="ln disclaimer_1">Tie.”<sup>†</sup></a></p></div>
				<ul class="ull ui-layout-horizontal ui-layout-left"><li><div class="parbase download section"><a class="dl_pdf" href="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Convertible/Model%20Overview/02_pdfs/MY13%20Camaro%20eBrochure_081612.pdf" target="_blank" id="" title="Download Catalog">Download Catalog</a>
	</div>
</li><li><div class="parbase download section"><a class="dl_pdf" href="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Coupe/Model%20Overview/02_pdfs/MY2013%20Camaro%20Spec%20Sheet_web.pdf" target="_blank" id="" title="Download Spec Sheet">Download Spec Sheet</a>
	</div>
</li></ul></div>
		</div></div>

</div>
<div class="parsys_cnt_well_2 parsys_list_c1"></div>
</div>
</div>
</div><div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"></div>

<div class="cnt_well_c1 section"><div class="mod modCnt_well_1 mds-cmp-content20" id="Performance">
	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					RUNS CIRCLES AROUND YOUR EXPECTATIONS</h2>
			</div></div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 15px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: -145px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Coupe/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-camaro-coupe-model-overview-performance-cnt-well-1-1280x475-01.jpg" alt="2013 Chevy Camaro Coupe Performance Car" width="1280" height="475" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Outstanding Performance and Efficiency</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Not only does the Camaro Coupe’s LFX V6 boast 323 horses that will propel you from 0 – 60 in 6.4 seconds. But it also offers impressive fuel efficiency: 30 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">highway<sup>†</sup></a> for the 6-speed automatic transmission 2LS.</p>
<p>The dual overhead cam engine gives you heart-racing performance. Direct Injection and Variable Valve Timing combine to ensure you’ll never waste a drop of gas. This is one high-tech, low-down, powerful engine. If unbridled power is what you’re after, the Camaro aluminum SS 6.2L V8 engine offers 426 horsepower and 420 lb.-ft. of torque befitting its aggressive reputation.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: -100px; margin-bottom: -100px; margin-left: -160px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Coupe/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-camaro-coupe-model-overview-performance-cnt-well-1-1726x570-02.png" alt="2013 Chevrolet Camaro Engine" width="726" height="570" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Suspension and Steering That Helps Keep You in Control</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    It’s so fun to drive, you might just volunteer to pick up the dry cleaning. The independent rear suspension and variable-ratio power steering give you the kind of handling you’ve only dreamt about. Its chassis is tuned to stick in turns and handle transitional situations like a champion. A 52/48 front-to-rear weight ratio gives you the kind of balance you’d expect from the world’s best sports cars.</p>
<p>  New in 2013 for manual transmission models is Hill Start Assist that will help keep your Camaro from rolling backwards when you’re taking off from an inclined position. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Performance from the Ground Up</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The exhilarating Camaro experience starts — literally — where the rubber meets the road. New 20” wheels available on LT and standard on SS, make a statement that’s impossible to ignore. Pair them with Pirelli<sup>®</sup> <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">PZero<sup>®†</sup></a> ultra high performance summer-only <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">tires<sup>†</sup></a> for a true experience of style and power.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 969px; top: 30px; margin-bottom: 30px; margin-left: -69px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Coupe/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-camaro-coupe-model-overview-performance-cnt-well-1-1129x300-03.jpg" alt="2013 Chevrolet Camaro Suspension and Steering" width="1129" height="300" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">

</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			The Power and Performance You’d Expect from a Camaro SS</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The first time you strap yourself into Camaro SS, make a mental note of where the hood release is. You’ll thank yourself later.</p>
<p>                    Because with this car you don’t just prop the hood to add windshield washer fluid. It’s packing an engine you’ll want to stand back and admire. And maybe let your friends sneak a peek at. If they’re lucky. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Unbridled Camaro Power…</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The 6.2L V8, paired with the standard 6-speed transmission, offers 426 horsepower and 420 lb.-ft. of torque. Or opt for the high-tech combination of speed and efficiency with the 6-speed automatic transmission with Active Fuel Management, which offers 24 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">highway<sup>†</sup></a> and delivers 400 horsepower.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			…and the Tools to Control It</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Launch control on the manual transmission SS helps control wheel spin for faster 0­-60 sprints. TAPshift<sup>®</sup> manual controls on the automatic transmission SS give you command over the gear selection for an exhilarating sports car experience, while keeping the transitions smooth.</p>
<p>The performance-tuned suspension with finely tuned stabilizer dampers provides an outstanding ride, balanced transitions, and excellent steering and handling. Pair it with the standard 20” wheels with <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">Pirelli<sup>®†</sup></a> PZero<sup>®</sup> ultra high performance summer-only <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">tires<sup>†</sup></a> and Brembo<sup>®</sup> brakes for superior performance and control.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">

	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			You’ll Feel It, They’ll Hear It</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    You’ll notice the electrically assisted power steering that is tuned for a specific feel and performance characteristics. It replaces traditional hydraulic power steering on Camaro SS.</p>
<p>  As for that sound they hear, that’s the ZL1-inspired, available dual-mode exhaust on Camaro SS. It enables peak performance at high engine speeds, and has been engineered to create an aggressive sound at idle without sounding overwhelming when cruising at a steady speed—the drawback of some aftermarket performance exhausts.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>

	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					THE 2013 CAMARO SS 1LE PERFORMANCE PACKAGE</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					Living Up to its Legendary Name</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>For more than two decades, both owners and enthusiasts have coveted the competition-ready third- and fourth-generation Camaro 1LE Performance Package. Now the 1LE is back, combining the white-knuckle performance elements of ZL1 and SS with a decidedly aggressive attitude of its own. Best of all, this 1LE is here to stay.</p>
<p>                    <a href="/culture/article/2013-camaro-family.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1+2col'});}">Learn more about the 1LE Performance Package.</a><br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>

<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			An Interior as Fine-Tuned as the Drive Itself</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Once you’re strapped in and ready for takeoff, you’ll notice that the Camaro Coupe interior is designed to make your rule of the road as comfortable and instinctive as possible. The comfort begins with the seats. Deep bolstered and ready for even the longest road trips, the LT, SS and ZL1 all come with standard six-way power driver and passenger seats.<br>
</p>
<p>But it’s the driver who really controls the Camaro Coupe, and nothing is more vital to that control than the steering wheel. <br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p><br>
Chevrolet engineers have optimized it to give you top-level response and control with a luxurious feel. Control audio functions with buttons right on the steering wheel, plus take advantage of the standard Bluetooth<sup>®</sup> wireless <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0" class="ln disclaimer_1">technology<sup>†</sup></a> for select phones that helps keep you connected while keeping your eyes on the road. You’ll also appreciate a new ZL1-inspired manual transmission shifter and a newly designed “frameless” inside rearview mirror that comes in handy to see all the vehicles you’ve left behind.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Gauge Your Performance</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The Driver Information Center has been designed to let you monitor  your vehicle’s vital stats at a glance so you can keep your eyes where  they belong — on the road.</p>
<p>From the intuitive instrument panel and  revised climate control graphics to a four-pack of auxiliary gauges —  standard on 2LT and 2SS — that includes oil pressure and transmission  temperature, you’ll always be up to date.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>

					CHEVROLET <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">MYLINK<sup>†</sup></a></h2>

<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Stay Connected, Informed and Entertained</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>With Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink,<sup>†</sup></a> every trip in your Camaro can feel like a getaway. Easily connect your smartphone with standard <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0" class="ln disclaimer_1">Bluetooth<sup>®†</sup></a> and take control of a wide range of top-notch technology right at your fingertips. Through voice commands or touch controls, tune into <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_13" class="ln disclaimer_1">Pandora<sup>®†</sup></a> or Stitcher <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_13" class="ln disclaimer_1">SmartRadio<sup>™†</sup></a> or listen to commercial-free programs through SiriusXM Satellite <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">Radio,<sup>†</sup></a> standard for 12 months on 2LT and 2SS models or three months LS, 1LT and 1SS models.<br>
<br>
&nbsp;
</p></div>

	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Head-Up Display</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Standard on 2LT and 2SS, the Head-Up Display (HUD) is specially designed  for high-performance driving situations. The HUD presents performance  data without requiring the driver to look away from the usual viewpoint.  HUD displays speed, rpm and more — even your radio station — right on  the windshield. You can even customize the display height and intensity  to best help you stay on top of vital information while keeping your  eyes on the road.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">

</p></div>

	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_1C_mobile_app.png" alt="" width="32" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									Mobile Apps</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Stay connected to your Camaro with the <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_5" class="ln disclaimer_1">myChevrolet<sup>†</sup> </a>or OnStar<sup>®</sup> <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">RemoteLink<sup>™†</sup></a> mobile apps. Start your <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_10" class="ln disclaimer_1">vehicle,<sup>†</sup></a> check diagnostics, contact roadside assistance, schedule routine maintenance and more. Available from the <a href="http://itunes.apple.com/us/app/mychevrolet/id398596699?mt=8" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://itunes.apple.com/us/app/mychevrolet/id398596699?mt=8');" target="_blank">iTunes Store</a> and <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.gm.chevrolet.nomad.ownership&feature=more_from_developer]" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.gm.chevrolet.nomad.ownership&feature=more_from_developer]');" target="_blank">Android Marketplace</a>.<br>

	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_1C_navigation_system.png" alt="" width="32" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									OnStar<sup>®</sup> Turn-by-Turn Navigation</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Have upcoming turns and street names displayed on the Driver Information Center or hear directions from the automated voice through <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_8" class="ln disclaimer_1">OnStar<sup>®</sup>,<sup>†</sup> </a>standard for the first six months. Or choose the available navigation radio for maps and directions downloaded to the new 7-inch diagonal touch-screen.</p></div>
				</div>
		</div></div>

	<div class="pf3c">

	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_1C_remote_start.png" alt="" width="32" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									Remote Start</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Press the button on your key fob and start your vehicle <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_10" class="ln disclaimer_1">remotely.<sup>†</sup></a> Requires available automatic transmission on LT and SS models.</p></div>

	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_siriusxm.png" alt="" width="92" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									SiriusXM Satellite Radio</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Enjoy a 12-month (2LT and SS models) or three-month trial (1LT and 1SS models) of SiriusXM Satellite <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">Radio<sup>†</sup></a> from coast to coast. <a href="http://www.siriusxm.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.siriusxm.com/');" target="_blank">See channel listings and more info</a>.<br>
</p></div>

	<div class="pf3b">

	<div class="text aoiw" id="">
				<h3 class="pt">
						<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared Resources/01_images/final_icons_4C_bluetooth.png" alt="" width="127" height="32" class="img"/><span>
									Wireless Technology</span>
							</h3>
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>                    Stepping into your car no longer means stepping away from your day. Take calls and connect your music with the touch of a <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">button,<sup>†</sup></a> available on select phones. </p></div>

	<h1 class="hl ">
						2013 HOT WHEELS SPECIAL EDITION</h1>	
				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						</div>
				</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Coupe/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-camaro-coupe-model-overview-specialedition-cnt-well-1-648x316-01.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="316" class="mm"/></div>

	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h3 class="pt">
					Full-Size Fun</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Available on either the Camaro 2LT or 2SS, and immediately recognizable as a Hot Wheels<sup>®</sup>-inspired Camaro with exterior features such as a vibrant Kinetic Blue Metallic paint scheme and 21&quot; red-striped wheels, this limited special edition is truly unique, as it’s the first-ever full-size production Hot Wheels car offered for sale by any manufacturer.</p>
<p>With production beginning in the first half of 2013, this new collaboration from Chevrolet and Hot Wheels holds great cultural significance, as the 1968 Custom Camaro 1:64-scale toy was one of the original sixteen Hot Wheels cars ever created. This rare opportunity to actually drive home a real-life Hot Wheels Camaro will be a dream come true for millions of fans and collectors alike.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>

	<div class="pf3a">

	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					WITH GREAT POWER COMES<br/>GREAT RESPONSIBILITY</h2>
			<h3 class="pt">
					First with Five in Every Category</h3>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>The 2013 Chevrolet Camaro Coupe has received the highest possible five-star score in every individual safety rating segment of the National Highway Traffic Safety Administration’s New Car Assessment <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_14" class="ln disclaimer_1">Program.<sup>†</sup></a></p>
<p><a href="/culture/article/vehicle-safety-preparation.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1+2col'});}">Learn more about the safety rating.</a></p>
<p>For Camaro, it’s high performance safety before, during and after a crash.<br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: -45px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Coupe/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-camaro-coupe-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-768x220-01.jpg" alt="2013 Chevrolet Camaro safety with OnStar" width="768" height="220" class="mm"/></div>


</div>

<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2013%20Camaro%20Coupe/Model%20Overview/01_images/2013-camaro-coupe-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-308x258-02.png" alt="6 Airbags for Camaro Coupe Performance Car Safety" width="308" height="258" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Before</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    Standard on every Camaro, antilock brakes and the StabiliTrak<sup>®</sup> Electronic Stability Control System with Traction Control help keep you in control during emergency maneuvers. The control module compares your steering input with the vehicle’s actual response and, if necessary, makes the corrections to help keep you on track.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			During</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    In the event of a collision, six standard <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_11" class="ln disclaimer_1">air bags<sup>†</sup></a> help protect heads, chests and knees. And the ultra-strength steel safety cage helps keep everyone in the vehicle protected.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			After</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p><a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2013-camaro-coupe_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_8" class="ln disclaimer_1">OnStar<sup>®†</sup></a> Automatic Crash Response, standard for the first six months on all Camaro models, means you can be automatically connected to emergency assistance if a crash occurs — whether or not the air bags deploy.<br>
</p>
<p><a href="/culture/article/vehicle-safety-preparation.html" onclick="if(typeof(Omniture_s) != 'undefined'){mrm.util.tagging.omniture_tl(this, this.href, 'o', undefined, {'prop27':'grid-1+2col'});}">Read more about Chevy vehicle safety </a></p></div>

	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					HOW SUSTAINABLE IS THE CAMARO?</h2>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Check out its “Ecologic” Features. Here at Chevrolet, we believe in being a responsible steward of our environment. Recently, we’ve developed a new way to communicate some of the environmentally significant features of each vehicle we make. We call it “Ecologic.”</p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05">
			<div class="inner">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/ecologic/2013-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-308x76-01.jpg" alt="" width="308" height="76" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Every aspect of Ecologic is audited by Two Tomorrows,  an independent third party sustainability auditor. To learn more about  Ecologic and the Two Tomorrows’ process, click here.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/ecologic/2013-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-648x315-02.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="315" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Fuel-Saving Technologies</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    On models with the 3.6L V6 engine, Continuously Variable Valve Timing (VVT) adjusts airflow in and out of the combustion chamber under all engine speeds, which makes for better fuel economy and lower emissions. With Direct Injection, fuel is injected directly into the combustion chamber in one of two ways; either before air flows into the cylinder or at the same time, resulting in efficient power generation and fuel consumption. </p>
<p>  </p>
<p>  On models with the 6.2L V8 engine, electric power steering uses an electric motor instead of an engine-driven belt, which results in a lighter overall workload and increased efficiency. Active Fuel Management™ deactivates fuel delivery to 4 cylinders in lighter-load conditions, such as highway cruising, which improves fuel economy (V8 SS, automatic transmission only).</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Responsible Manufacturing</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    The engine facilities are landfill-free. These facilities use a process to reuse, recycle or convert to energy all waste created in their daily operations, which conserves resources. Some water and engine-air deflectors are manufactured with more than 99% recycled content, which includes used tires. Recycled material conserves resources and reduces landfill deposits. </p>
<p>  </p>
<p>  Landfill gas supplies 16% of the energy to heat and cool the Toledo, OH, transmission facility (automatic transmission only), which makes the facility less reliant on fossil fuels. The facility also features a designated habitat area certified by the Wildlife Habitat Council, which provides ecological benefits.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			End-of-Life Recyclability</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    After the vehicle’s useful life, 85% of it is recyclable. The majority of its components can be broken down and recycled, which conserves resources and reduces landfill deposits. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
